				<section data-particle_enable="false" data-particle-mobile-disabled="false" class="elementor-section elementor-top-section elementor-element elementor-element-4103597 elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default elementor-invisible" data-id="4103597" data-element_type="section" data-settings="{&quot;animation&quot;:&quot;fadeInUp&quot;,&quot;_ha_eqh_enable&quot;:false}">
						<div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default">
					<div class="elementor-column elementor-col-100 elementor-top-column elementor-element elementor-element-6ac48ba" data-id="6ac48ba" data-element_type="column">
			<div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated">
						<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-8d627ce elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="8d627ce" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
			<h1 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">INTRODUCTION</h1>		</div>
				</div>
				<div class="elementor-element elementor-element-cb285df elementor-widget elementor-widget-ha-unfold happy-addon ha-unfold happy-addon-pro" data-id="cb285df" data-element_type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;unfold_text&quot;:&quot;Read More&quot;,&quot;fold_text&quot;:&quot;Read Less&quot;,&quot;trigger&quot;:&quot;click&quot;,&quot;fold_height&quot;:100,&quot;transition_duration&quot;:500,&quot;unfold_icon&quot;:{&quot;value&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;library&quot;:&quot;&quot;},&quot;fold_icon&quot;:{&quot;value&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;library&quot;:&quot;&quot;}}" data-widget_type="ha-unfold.default">
				<div class="elementor-widget-container">
					<div class="ha-unfold-widget-wrapper">
						<div class="ha-unfold-data">
				<div class="ha-unfold-data-render">
					<p><span style="color: #009; font-family: bazooka;">SZABIST</span>&#8211;<span style="color: #009; font-family: Stag Stencil;">ZABTech (iTVE) </span>was founded in the year 2000 with the objective of providing high-quality technical and vocational education. Its primary goal is to develop a skilled national workforce that can actively contribute to the economic and social progress of the country. 
<p><span style="color: #009; font-family: bazooka;">SZABIST</span>&#8211;<span style="color: #009; font-family: Stag Stencil;">ZABTech (iTVE) </span>has its Directorate in Karachi and operates state-of-the-art technical and vocational education training institutes across various locations in <b>Sindh</b> and now expended to <b>Baluchistan</b>. 
<p>Currently, there are <b>9 (Nine) permanent institutes situated in Hyderabad, Larkana, Shaheed Benazirabad,  Tando Muhammad Khan, Thatta(Gharo),  Sehwan(Jamshoro), Mirpur Khas, Karachi and HUB(Balochistan).</b> These institutes hold accreditation from organizations such as the National and Vocational Technical Training Commission of Pakistan (NAVTTC), Sindh TEVTA, Sindh Trade Testing Board (TTB).</p>

<p>Additionally, <span style="color: #009; font-family: bazooka;">SZABIST</span>&#8211;<span style="color: #009; font-family: Stag Stencil;">ZABTech (iTVE) </span> is also accredited with renowned international institutes such as City &amp; Guilds (UK). This accreditation further enhances the credibility and global recognition of our programs, ensuring that students receive education and certifications that are recognized and valued internationally.</p>

<p><span style="color: #009; font-family: bazooka;">SZABIST</span>&#8211;<span style="color: #009; font-family: Stag Stencil;">ZABTech (iTVE) </span> provides study opportunities in <b>four sectors 1. Information Technology (IT), 2. Manufacturing, 3. Service and 4. Constructions.</b> This allows learners to choose the program that aligns with their employment prospects most effectively.</p>

<p>In accordance with various projects requirements and the goal of skill development for youth, <span style="color: #009; font-family: bazooka;">SZABIST</span>&#8211;<span style="color: #009; font-family: Stag Stencil;">ZABTech (iTVE) </span> has established satellite units at the union council and village level. These units are designed to provide training directly to the community, making skills accessible to all young individuals. This initiative follows the approach of skills for all, ensuring that no one is left behind in acquiring valuable skills.</p>

<p><span style="color: #009; font-family: bazooka;">SZABIST</span>&#8211;<span style="color: #009; font-family: Stag Stencil;">ZABTech (iTVE) </span> prioritizes employability in a competitive environment and provides opportunities for entrepreneurship. Our all chapters are proud to offer outstanding facilities, including well-equipped workshops, computer labs, business incubation, simulators for hands on practical work, and incubators for different trades. These resources enable students to gain practical, hands-on workplace based training.</p>

<p><span style="color: #009; font-family: bazooka;">SZABIST</span>&#8211;<span style="color: #009; font-family: Stag Stencil;">ZABTech (iTVE) </span>, believes in the power of collaboration and practical training to empower individuals so that they can contribute to the growth of industries.</p>
 Creating opportunities for young individuals and cultivating a skilled workforce through our efforts in establishing partnerships and organizing job fairs. By facilitating these interactions, our aim is to bridge the gap between job seekers and Industries, which ultimately leading to successful employment outcomes for our youth.</p>
				</div>
			</div>

				(function($) {
                    "use strict";

                    var target = $('.elementor-element-2738304');

                    
                    var EaelParallaxElement = {

						init: function() {
							elementorFrontend.hooks.addAction('frontend/element_ready/global', EaelParallaxElement.initWidget);
						},
                        responsiveParallax: function(){
                            var android = 1,
                                ios = 1;
                            switch( true || 1 ){
                                case android && ios:
                                    return /iPad|iPhone|iPod|Android/;
                                    break;
                                case android && ! ios:
                                    return /Android/;
                                    break;
                                case ! android && ios:
                                    return /iPad|iPhone|iPod/;
                                    break;
                                case ( ! android && ! ios ):
                                    return null;
                            }
                        },
						initWidget: function( $scope ) {

							target.jarallax({
								type: 'scroll',
								speed: 1.3,
								keepImg: true,
                                disableParallax: EaelParallaxElement.responsiveParallax(),
							});
						}

					};

					$( window ).on('elementor/frontend/init', EaelParallaxElement.init);
